linguas="af am ar as ast az be be@latin bg bn bn_IN br bs ca ca@valencia cmn crh cs cy da de dz el en_AU en_CA en_GB en_US en@shaw eo es et eu fa fi fr fur fy ga gl gu gv ha he hi hr hu hy ia id ig io is it ja ka kk km kn ko ku ky li lt lv mai mg mi mk ml mn mr ms nb nds ne nl nn nso oc or pa pl ps pt pt_BR ro ru rw si sk sl sq sr sr@latin sr@ije sv ta te th tk tr ug uk ur uz uz@cyrillic vi wa xh yi yo zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW zu "; \
for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/tmp/caja-gtk3/pkg/caja-gtk3/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/caja-gtk3/src/caja-1.10.4/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/caja.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/caja.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/caja.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/caja.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/caja.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/caja.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/caja.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/caja.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
